		function genUID() {
			const crypto = window['crypto'] || window['msCrypto'] || false;
			if (crypto && crypto.randomUUID) {
				return crypto.randomUUID();
			} else if (crypto && crypto.getRandomValues) {
				return ([1e7]+-1e3+-4e3+-8e3+-1e11).replace(/[018]/g, function(c) {
					return (c ^ crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(1))[0] & 15 >> c / 4).toString(16);
				});
			}

			return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
				const r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
				return v.toString(16);
			});
		}
		function getCookie(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');

<td colspan="5" class="Nptable-ocbody">Increases own NP damage for 1 turn. <span title="This effect activates first before dealing damage." style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;"><i>(Activates first)</i></span> <img alt="UpgradeIconText" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="13" data-image-name="UpgradeIconText.png" data-image-key="UpgradeIconText.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/fategrandorder/images/7/75/UpgradeIconText.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/15?cb=20171224084823" class="lazyload"><br>Increases party's NP generation rate for 3 turns.
</td></tr>

<th>Bond 10 Craft Essence
</th>
<td colspan="3"><span class="craft_essence_icon"><a href="/wiki/Certain_Truth_and_Death" title="Certain Truth and Death"><img alt="CEIcon789" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="75" height="82" data-image-name="CEIcon789.webp" data-image-key="CEIcon789.webp" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/fategrandorder/images/8/8f/CEIcon789.webp/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/75?cb=20230325133637" class="lazyload"></a></span>
</td>
<td colspan="7"><b><a href="/wiki/Certain_Truth_and_Death" title="Certain Truth and Death">Certain Truth and Death</a></b><br>When equipped on <strong class="mw-selflink selflink">Avicebron</strong>:<br><img alt="Artsupstatus" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="25" height="25" data-image-name="Artsupstatus.png" data-image-key="Artsupstatus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/fategrandorder/images/d/d7/Artsupstatus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/25?cb=20220103123625" class="lazyload"> Increases party's Arts performance by 10%,<br><img alt="Busterupstatus" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="25" height="25" data-image-name="Busterupstatus.png" data-image-key="Busterupstatus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/fategrandorder/images/a/ad/Busterupstatus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/25?cb=20220103121517" class="lazyload"> Increases party's Buster performance by 10%<br>while self is on the field.
</td></tr>

<td style="width:45%;padding:0;vertical-align:top;overflow:hidden;"><div class="tabber wds-tabber"><div class="wds-tabs__wrapper with-bottom-border"><ul class="wds-tabs"><li class="wds-tabs__tab wds-is-current" data-hash="NA"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">NA</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="TL"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">TL</a></div></li></ul></div><div class="wds-tab__content wds-is-current"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>NA Localization:</b></span>
His real full name is Solomon ben Yehuda ibn Gabirol. He was an eleventh-century philosopher, poet, and practitioner of a particular form of magecraft called Kabbalah.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div><div class="wds-tab__content"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>Fan Translation:</b></span>
His real name is Solomon ben Judah ibn Gabirol. A philosopher, poet and a kabbalist of the 11th century that employs one of the main genres of magecraft, the Kabbalah.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div></div>

<th style="width:10%;padding-left:10px;">Bond 2
</th>
<td style="width:45%;padding-left:10px;overflow:hidden;" lang="ja">???????<br>
<p>??????<br>
?????<br>
????????<br>
?????????<br>
????<br>
???????????<br>
?????????<br>
?????????<br>
??????

</td>
<td style="width:45%;padding:0;vertical-align:top;overflow:hidden;"><div class="tabber wds-tabber"><div class="wds-tabs__wrapper with-bottom-border"><ul class="wds-tabs"><li class="wds-tabs__tab wds-is-current" data-hash="NA"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">NA</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="TL"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">TL</a></div></li></ul></div><div class="wds-tab__content wds-is-current"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>NA Localization:</b></span>
A Caster and skilled golem keeper who established the discipline of Kabbalah, which is one of the foundations for magecraft.<br>
Golems can be produced in factories, but to do so requires careful long-term planning and a vast budget (enough to drive a normal mage to bankruptcy ten times over). Still, the resulting golems are about as powerful as an E-rank Servant, and can be manufactured endlessly as long as the budget permits.<br>
However, Avicebron can summon golems of his own accord in battle, though these can only be used temporarily, and are not especially durable.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div><div class="wds-tab__content"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>Fan Translation:</b></span>
Being a user of the magical foundation of the Kabbalah, he is a Caster specialised in the minting of golems.<br>
Although merely building a golem-minting workshop already requires of him enough budget and long hours of work to make an average magus go bankrupt ten times over, the golems that he mints have the same level of power as an E Rank Servant, and he can produce them infinitely as long as the budget lasts.<br>
However, the golems that appear during regular combat are temporary articles to be employed in that combat alone, and have no endurance at all.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div></div>
</td></tr>

<p><span style="display:none;"><b>NA Localization:</b></span>
Tranquil Fig: EX<br>
One legend says that a man, jealous of Avicebron's poetic gifts, killed him and buried him at the foot of a fig tree. Curious why the tree bore such extraordinarily sweet fruit, the people of the surrounding area decided to investigate. This is what brought the murderer's crime to light.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div><div class="wds-tab__content"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

<p><span style="display:none;"><b>Fan Translation:</b></span>
<b><a href="/wiki/Fig_Tree_of_Tranquility" title="Fig Tree of Tranquility">Fig Tree of Tranquility</a>: EX</b><br>
According to legends, he was killed by a certain man that was jealous of his poetic gifts and buried under the roots of a fig tree.<br>
It has been said that people became marvelled by the unique sweetness of its fruits, eventually digging it up and exposing the man's sins.
</p>

<td style="width:45%;padding:0;vertical-align:top;overflow:hidden;"><div class="tabber wds-tabber"><div class="wds-tabs__wrapper with-bottom-border"><ul class="wds-tabs"><li class="wds-tabs__tab wds-is-current" data-hash="NA"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">NA</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="TL"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">TL</a></div></li></ul></div><div class="wds-tab__content wds-is-current"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>NA Localization:</b></span>
Golem Keter Malkuth?<br>
Rank: A+<br>
NP Type: Anti-Army<br>
Range: 1 - 10<br>
Maximum Targets: 100<br>
Royal Crown, Light of Wisdom.<br>
A Noble Phantasm that remained unfinished during Caster's lifetime.<br>
An autonomous Reality Marble that replicates the Primordial Man, Adam, and can continuously repaint the world so long as it exists. However, as with regular golems, certain materials are required for it to maintain its existence.<br>
The giant wields an obsidian sword, and can continue to function even after Caster's death, as long as its feet touch the ground to grant it the blessing of the earth.<br>
A mage must be used to serve as the golem's core, and the core's power and compatibility both affect the giant's strength.<br>
As a side note, the giant is only about fifteen meters tall when first constructed, but with the magical energy supplied from the earth, it can grow beyond thirty or even sixty meters.<br>
The giant eventually turns into the Garden of Eden itself, transforming the entire world into a peaceful, tranquil place.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div><div class="wds-tab__content"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>Fan Translation:</b></span>
<b>Royal Crown, the Light of Wisdom</b><br>
<b>Rank:</b> A+<br>
<b>Type:</b> Anti-Army<br>
<b>Range:</b> 110<br>
<b>Maximum Targets:</b> 100 people<br>
Golem Keter Malkuth.<br>
An incomplete Noble Phantasm that Caster was unable to create in his lifetime.<br>
An imitation of the "original human (Adam)", this autonomous Reality Marble continues to repaint the world so long it exists.<br>
However, it requires raw materials that exist in reality - just like all other golems.<br>
It continues to work even if Caster - its creator - were to perish and, so long its feet remain connected to the ground, it will never be destroyed thanks to a blessing from the Earth.<br>
Its weapon is an obsidian sword.<br>
In addition, it requires a single magus in its central section to act as a reactor core,<br>
This giant's strength will vary in accordance with the strength, compatibility of said reactor core.<br>
Furthermore, although its initial materials make for 15 meters at best, it will gradually enlarge to 30, 60 meters by means of prana supply from the Earth.<br>
Eventually, this giant will probably become paradise itself and transform the entire world into a gentle, peaceful place.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div></div>
</td></tr>

<td style="width:45%;padding-left:10px;overflow:hidden;" lang="ja">???????????<br>
<p>??????????????<br>
?????????<br>
???????<br><br>
?????????????????????????????????????????????????????????<br>
???????????????????????????????????<br><br>

</td>
<td style="width:45%;padding:0;vertical-align:top;overflow:hidden;"><div class="tabber wds-tabber"><div class="wds-tabs__wrapper with-bottom-border"><ul class="wds-tabs"><li class="wds-tabs__tab wds-is-current" data-hash="NA"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">NA</a></div></li><li class="wds-tabs__tab" data-hash="TL"><div class="wds-tabs__tab-label"><a href="#">TL</a></div></li></ul></div><div class="wds-tab__content wds-is-current"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>NA Localization:</b></span>
He is likely to be difficult to deal with as a Caster-class Servant. That should, however, be both expected and understandable if you accept the fact that he would readily trample anyone in service of fulfilling his dream.<br><br>
He was a sickly man during his lifetime, particularly prone to skin infections. In consequence, he was said to have been dour and pessimistic. His refusal to take off his mask and reveal his face reflects that particular quality. Historically, Avicebron is said to have passed down his philosophical teachings from Arabia to Europe. It may not even be a stretch to say that he was one of the first to begin the Renaissance.<br><br>
He also coined the term Kabbalah, which is derived from the Hebrew word for "receive." Legend has it that he created a female golem to do housework for him.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div><div class="wds-tab__content"><p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p><div style="padding:0 10px;">
<p><span style="display:none;"><b>Fan Translation:</b></span>
As a Servant Caster, he is likely a type that is difficult to handle.<br>
It should be possible to understand that this is also due a side of his that mercilessly tramples anyone underfoot so long it is for the sake of realising his dream.<br><br>
Having a poor health, he often suffered from some sort of illness - among which a skin disease was particularly serious. Maybe because of that, it has been said that he was gloomy and pessimistic. In this work, one can peek in his heart by the manner how he never takes off his mask to show his face.<br>
In actual history, Avicebron became known across Arabia and Europe thanks to his philosophical thoughts. <br>
In a sense, it could be also said that he supported the Renaissance culture.<br><br>
Also, he invented the term "Kabbalah" from the Hebraic word for "to receive".<br>
In legends, it has also been said that he minted a female-type golem for the sake of performing daily housework.
</p>
</div><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p></div></div>

It was the right choice, at the time. He was so sure of it.

<td style="width:45%;padding-left:10px;overflow:hidden;">Teacher-Type Servant<br>
<p>A masked scholar who controls an army of golems. His dream is to create an all-powerful giant robot. He seems pretty mild-mannered, but won't hesitate to make terrible sacrifices in pursuit of his goals. Frankly, he's a bit of a sociopath.
